## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics (continuous-time growth models)
**Analysis**: The target is a population time-derivative dP_dt driven by current population size P and possibly explicit time t, matching classical continuous-time demographic/ecological growth laws (density-independent, density-dependent, Allee effects, harvesting, and time-varying forcing).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Malthusian (exponential) growth ODE: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent per-capita growth)
- Linear birth–death with immigration/emigration: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 (net per-capita growth plus constant influx/outflux)
- Power-law (allometric) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (nonlinear scaling of growth rate with population size)
- Self-limiting quadratic mortality: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 (crowding/competition producing a carrying capacity)
- Verhulst (logistic) ODE form: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density dependence with carrying capacity ~ 1/c1)
- Theta-logistic (generalized density dependence): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (flexible concavity of density dependence)
- Gompertz growth ODE: dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 - log(P)) (per-capita growth decreases approximately linearly with log P)
- Richards-type generalized logistic ODE: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)**c3 (extra shape control for approach to carrying capacity)
- Strong Allee effect (bistability): dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 * P - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (negative growth at low P, positive at intermediate P, negative near carrying capacity)
- Logistic with constant harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (removal at fixed rate; can induce extinction threshold)
- Saturating per-capita growth (crowding-limited births): dP_dt = (c0 * P) / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P (births saturate with P; linear deaths)
- Seasonally forced growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t + c3)) - c4 * P**2 (periodic environment modulating growth plus density dependence)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Check per-capita growth g(P,t) = dP_dt / P: if g is ~constant → exponential-like; if g decreases with P → density dependence.
- Carrying capacity corresponds to a positive root of dP_dt(P)=0 where slope d(dP_dt)/dP is negative (stable equilibrium).
- Quadratic or higher-order negative terms in P (e.g., -P^2, -P^(1+theta)) indicate crowding/competition; the exponent controls how sharply growth shuts off.
- Presence of a factor (c*P - 1) multiplying P suggests an Allee threshold (growth negative below P≈1/c).
- A log(P) term in dP_dt (e.g., P*(c - log P)) indicates multiplicative, proportional regulation typical of Gompertz-type dynamics (linear decline in per-capita growth vs log-size).
- An additive negative constant term in dP_dt suggests constant harvesting/removal; this can create a critical population size even if density dependence is mild.
- Explicit periodic dependence on t (sin/cos terms) suggests seasonal forcing; expect oscillations in growth rate even if P is smooth.
- If dP_dt includes both linear +P and nonlinear -P^k terms, early-time dynamics are near-exponential (linear dominates), late-time dynamics are regulation-limited (nonlinear dominates).

## GT Analysis

The GT is:
```
0.13870625668024555*(-1 + P/8.038138014396704)*(1 - P/70.01799944958296)*P + 0.13870625668024555*(1 - P/70.01799944958296)*P + 0.13870625668024555*P/(1 + exp(-8.038138014396704*(-0.5894251550796137 + P)))
```

Let me simplify. Let me denote α = 0.1387..., a = 8.0381..., b = 70.018..., d = 0.5894...

**Term 1:** α*(-1 + P/a)*(1 - P/b)*P
**Term 2:** α*(1 - P/b)*P  
**Term 3:** α*P/(1 + exp(-a*(-d + P)))

Combine Terms 1 and 2:
α*(1 - P/b)*P * [(-1 + P/a) + 1] = α*(1 - P/b)*P * (P/a)
= α*P²/(a*b) * (b - P) = (α/a) * P² * (1 - P/b)

Wait, let me redo:
α*(1 - P/b)*P*(P/a) = (α/a)*P²*(1 - P/b) = (α/a)*P² - (α/(a*b))*P³

So Terms 1+2 = (α/a)*P² - (α/(a*b))*P³

**Term 3:** α*P/(1 + exp(-a*(P - d))) — this is a sigmoid-scaled term.

So GT = -(α/(a*b))*P³ + (α/a)*P² + α*P*σ(a*(P-d))

where σ is the sigmoid function.

The GT has these basis functions:
- P³ (cubic term)
- P² (quadratic term)  
- P * sigmoid(a*(P-d)) — a sigmoid-weighted linear term

This is a **cubic polynomial in P** plus a **sigmoid-modulated P term**. The GT also depends only on P, not on t.

1. GT has NO dependence on t. Any candidate with t-dependence that can't be zeroed out is NO MATCH.

The sigmoid function α*P/(1+exp(-a*(P-d))) cannot be represented by:
- sin(c*log(P*c+1)+c) — these are oscillatory
- P*c/(P*c+1) — this is a rational function, not sigmoid
- exp(P*c) — exponential
- log(P*c+1) — logarithmic

**None of the candidates contain a sigmoid function.** The sigmoid σ(x) = 1/(1+exp(-x)) is a fundamentally different basis function from sin, cos, log, rational functions, or simple exponentials.
